<review>I have been a patient of Dr. Chiang's for 6 years now. Finding a dentist who is truly passionate about helping others and doing what is right is no easy feat. Many dentists do not take the time to get to know you, fully understand the problems you're experiencing, and share knowledge/research on best practices in dentistry. Dr. Chiang is, by far, the most ethical, honest, and skilled dentist I've ever had.

Dr. Chiang recently moved into her own office that is incredibly warm, inviting, and easy to access. Nestled in with many other doctor offices, the areas is quiet, charming, and relaxing. Even through all the COVID measures, Dr. Chiang's team is friendly, communicative, and timely in their responses to the evolving crisis. The office is equipped with an amazing air filtration system through the whole office and the team is in full PPE. There was not a single moment where I felt uncomfortable or concerned about my health (my last visit was on 7/25/20). They check your temperature with a super neat device that is contact free - how neat!

Dr. Chiang has helped me learn SO much about how to properly take care of my teeth (based on their unique characteristics). Dr. Chiang introduced me to a new floss, drTungs, that works SO MUCH BETTER than any other floss I've used (truth be told I was not much of a flosser before going to Dr. Chiang). I've recommended it to more than 20 of my friends who now all use the product too. Further, Dr. Chiang noticed my teeth have been wearing down over the years and diagnose my teeth grinding. Now I wear a night guard that helps protect my teeth from the chipping that was beginning to happen.

Lastly, I must name that I specifically travel from Concord, CA for my appointments with Dr. Chiang because of the excellence in service & care that I receive. Yes, that means driving over 2 hours with CA traffic at times, yet it's worth it. I went in for my cleaning this morning.
I have education in the medical field so I am very particular about infection risk. I am not an essential worker so though I have had low exposure risk, I feel very stressed about COVID and have been very careful. I only exercise in the morning, I clean my groceries and packages, and I wear a mask, cotton gloves, and glasses everywhere. I get delivery of most groceries.
I asked Dr. Chiang and Elise multiple questions about their infection protocol. They answered patiently by email.
They gave a special hepa filter for dental work. All staff wear PPE of gowns, double masks, face shields, and gloves. The staff put on masks before they enter the building. They have multiple sanitizer stations.
I waited in the car and called when I arrived. I was asked to come in masked. I was asked to wash my hands and demask only immediately before my procedure. I swished peroxide mouthwash for one minute. I then sat in the treatment chair. The special filter ran the whole time. After procedure, I re-masked and washed my hands and then paid at the front desk with Apple Pay. It all ran so smoothly.
Dr. Chiang runs a tight ship! I feel safe at this practice.</Review>

<Pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNgdQttV3CPRiY7fbK8VVzDlkd0GqiiF3aqDm5r=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]<//Pictures><Time>1555779375570<//Time>< username>
Joe Murray< /username>
<text>UPDATE April 2019: Recently returned and was happy to find Noon open. A couple of weeks back it was closed at lunch. They did not answer the phone a day or two later. I thought they folded.

There was less on the menu than before. I chose The Burger, a strange choice in this place. It was quickly placed in the Top Three burgers of all time.

Deliberate. That's the word. This thing was constructed and assembled with purpose. Purpose being flavor and texture. The pattie at first appeared hyper shaped and cylindrical (like a frozen pattie) but it was the best part. As it should be right? Cooked just beyond rare, perfectly pink, not raw, and beefy tasting. Then the flavor road -first the cheese. Not sure what kind, but dairy umph and tang. Then the crunch of greens including sliced fennel for a garden blast. The jalapeÃ±os added some heat at the right time. A sauce seasoned just right. And the sesame bun pulled it together just before gulping down the bite. Yum. "It was like the chef put it together like this on purpose. Deliberate."

No squeezing out of sauce or toppings. No overly wide TMJ inducing height. Beef forward overall. Go try it.

And re: the reduced menu... As a fan of Kitchen Nightmares I take this of a sign of tight kitchen and restaurant management. They know what sells and what tastes good. Might be a communication issue to let customers know they are (or maybe are not) rotating the menu items regularly.

Go back and try it again. Enjoy a walk in the always sunny neighborhood.
###

Aprill/May 2018:Discovered this new place on a walk around Esprit Park. Tasty cookie and capacino.< /text>< user>

< review>
Noon All Day is a nourishing oasis, with food as comfy as a hug, prepared with such creativity and care.

The service is perfection - they anticipate your needs, bringing elevated service to a casual setting. Everyone there seems so thrilled to be a part of Noon!

Order a Sightglass coffee and a pastry - they are a must! Noon's croissants and danishes are creative & flavorful - complementary to their menu. I ordered the seasonal ricotta danish. A crisp buttery delight, with creamy herb ricotta. Many of their sweet pastries look like they are straight out of Marie Antoinette and they are surprisingly light, with many creative ways to cut the richness, and keep things on the lighter side.

The portions of their main dishes are perfect - large enough to satisfy, without feelin too full. I recommend ordering many plates to share so you can taste it all. (My favorites are the socca, the pocket sandwich, the nougat yogurt pistachio pastry, the scotch olives, their pickled veggies, and all of their essentials to add to any dish). Noon is a great place to order a variety of small and big items for sharing, whether that be for brunch, a mid-afternoon snack, or a dinner date. (You can add a poached egg to anything on the menu, for brunch too!)

You need to visit this gem of a restaurant, see for yourself.

PS Noon is the ultimate location to take some Twin Peaks pictures (their tile looks similar to the Black Lodge flooring.)</review>

<userid>104380474517690904906<//userid><name>Raquel Mata<//name><Time>1619757836726</Time><Rate>4< /Rate>< review>
1st time that I tried this place and it was awesome and delish! So you can order either a regular bowl, superbowl or combo (which is a regular bowl + rice &drink). You order your meat then add whatever veggies you want, you pick your choice of sauce then they add the noodle and grill it. I cant believe how much food there was. The styrofoam box was overflowing. The only downside is there were only 3 people in the whole foodchain. The cashier who also preps your food, the chef, and another guy inside who refills the food outside as needed. A little slow service for a place when its busy. But either way, the mongolian food but worth the wait!</review>

< Text>
This place is okay. When I heard that there was a Mongolian Grill in the area I got excited and went there right away. To my disappointment it is NOT a typical Mongolian Grill. The toppings are skimpy, so are the sauces. The noodles are not typical egg noodles. And they charge top dollar for only 1 bowl, where as most Mongolian Grills are all-you-can-eat with a drink for $9.95. If you want a one bowl with rice and a drink be prepared to spend $11. All that said, if you need a fix of Mongolian food and cannot travel far, this place will suffice until they bring a solid franchise to the area.</Text>

<rating>3< /rating>< text>
We visit Jane quite often for good food and a pleasant environment. The bar is good, with a sure hand and eye producing fine cocktails.
On this occasion though, it became apparent that there were a few flaws.  I had the veal marsala and my wife had the special Hawaiian swordfish.  Whilst both were tasty, the basic flavors of the meat and fish were completely shrouded by the sauces.  My veal could have been almost any light meat, the swordfish any firm fish. As I said, tasty, but a bit of a let down.
The desert, a semi-freddo with caramel was delicious,  but not a semi-fredo.
We'll go back, but without great expectations.</text>

<Name>Mccauley Rocha<//Name><UserId.>110635643184041676815<//UserId.><Review>Though my experience at Jane at the Marketplace has been mostly positive, today in celebration of my sister's birthday...I have a few exceptions.
First of all I must say that our server, Catherine did a very good job. She was cheery, and informative. Ditto the dude in charge running the front end.
I have always liked the environment here: big space, cloth napery and good quality glass and cutlery. A mid priced  restaurant with the class to fill the space with touches that make a difference in our overall enjoyment.
There were 4 of us today and we ordered:
Med Pizza
Blackened plank Salmon with french fries and Mango/Citrus coulis
Turkey Cobb with Gorgonzola
Red Onion Rings
Coconut Cake
Last time here i ordered the (i assume) Special Pizza which was a pretty spectacular Prosciutto, Mushrooms on a white, cheese sauce. A very delicious item. (i've attached a photo of this pizza to this review along with the Med pizza)
This Med Pizza was a major disappointment. The crust was lifeless and tasteless and was an odd tan color: as it it were whole wheat which it doesn't seem to be based on the menu description. Something was off with this dough: not leavened enough? Leavened too much?
The Buffalo Mozz was good but there just wasn't enough Olive tapenade to make an impression. Worst of all, the greens were dry when they should have been dressed. Even dressed with just olive oil, salt and pepper. Where was the Balsamic?
My sister very much enjoyed the Salmon and found the Mango/Citrus  sauce a tasty accompaniment to the fish. The Salmon was of excellent quality and grilled as ordered. A very good dish.
The Turkey Cobb was good: all of the accoutrements were prepared very well though the Gorgonzola pieces were ridiculously big. Odd to be sure. Also the Turkey was good: obviously not deli turkey but either bought or cooked in house. The greens were crispy and fresh.
The Firestone Red Onion Rings are once again pretty perfect: light, well seasoned batter but also fried very very well. This item is a prime example of a simple dish elevated to ultra goodness because all of the pieces are handled with care and in a careful, thoughtful manner.
The Coconut Cake arrived with a candle which was unlit and no one from the staff to sing Happy Birthday. Huh? a 200 buck lunch ($50 check average for each of us 4) and no one could spare the time?
Despite that, this cake is as coco-nutty as you can get. The cake itself was tender, fluffy and redolent of coconut . Both the buttercream and filling were delicious. The portion of cake sits in a milk-style sauce jam packed with coconut flavor. No artificial coconut "extracts" in sight or in the taste of this cake!
I can see  why people love this item.< /Review></record></dataset><record>

Imagine my frustration at this point...

I shopped around a bit on October 5th and didn't really find anything I liked enough and was ready to give up and wait out this next delivery date. My boyfriend had purchased a couch from Andrew's a while back and told me to just give them a call to see if they could help. I called October 6th and I got an answer from Michael even though they were closed that day.
